#### Ancestral Cry (13)
- **Tags**: Warcry
- **Class**: Skill Gems
- **Requires**: Requires: Level (1—90), (4—157) Str
- **Description**: Perform a Warcry using Glory gained by Igniting enemies to turn you into an embodiment of Kaom. While embodying Kaom, you Trigger Volcanic Steps while travelling, Melee Strikes and Slams are Ancestrally Boosted, and your Melee Strikes Trigger Volcanic Eruption.

#### Boneshatter (1)
- **Tags**: Attack
- **Class**: One Hand Maces
- **Requires**: Requires: Level (1—90), (4—157) Str
- **Description**: Attack enemies with a melee Strike. The Strike will cause a Heavy Stun on enemies that are Primed for Stun. Upon causing a Heavy Stun it will also create a Shockwave, dealing a large amount of damage in an area.
- **Implicit**: Your Boneshatter becomes a Celestial Effect.
- **Mods**: +2 to Melee Strike Range | While Dual Wielding, both weapons hit with 30% less damage | Cannot cause Stun buildup | Shockwave radius is 2 metres | 50% more damage with Hits for Shockwaves originating / from a Unique enemy | active skill show crush range [1] | crushing blow [1] | melee conditional step distance [17] | precise cursor targeting uses contact point height offset [1] | display statset hide usage stats [1] | is area damage [1]

#### Earthshatter (7)
- **Tags**: Attack
- **Class**: One Hand Maces
- **Requires**: Requires: Level (1—90), (4—157) Str
- **Description**: Slam the ground, sending out a fissure that deals area damage to enemies it passes under and thrusts a spike from the ground when it ends. Warcries performed near the spike will cause it to shatter, damaging surrounding enemies.
- **Implicit**: Your Earthshatter becomes a Verdant Effect. | Your Earthshatter becomes a Molten Effect. | Your Earthshatter becomes a Kitava Effect.
- **Mods**: While Dual Wielding, both weapons hit with / 30% less attack speed | Deals damage along the fissure's path and in a / 1 metre radius around the emerging spike | Spike duration is 6 seconds | Limit 6 Spikes | Maximum 6 Spikes | Explosion radius is 2 metres | is area damage [1] | base skill effect duration [6000]

#### Forge Hammer (9)
- **Tags**: Attack
- **Class**: One Hand Maces
- **Requires**: Requires: Level (1—90), (4—157) Str
- **Description**: Hurl a fiery hammer that Slams into the ground and lodges there. While the hammer is lodged in the ground, reusing this Skill recalls the hammer and resets the Skill's cooldown. Alternatively, using a Warcry near the lodged hammer causes it to shatter, releasing a number of Molten Fissures in a spiral.
- **Mods**: Converts 30% of Physical damage to Fire damage | While Dual Wielding, both weapons hit with 30% less damage | Impact radius is 1.8 metres | Hammer duration is 12 seconds | Cooldown does not recover while the hammer is lodged | Converts 100% of Physical damage to Fire damage | Cooldown does not recover during Buff effect | Fissure duration is 8 seconds | Limit 10 Fissures | 70% more Attack Speed | attack maximum action distance + [40] | can perform skill while moving [1] | forge hammer base maximum number of fissures [10] | forge hammer base number of fissures [5] | forge hammer hammer speed [300] | forge hammer maximum hammers [1] | is area damage [1] | movement speed +% final while performing action [-70] | movement speed acceleration +% per second while performing action [160] | movement speed while performing action locked duration % [50] | active skill base area of effect radius [10] | display statset hide usage stats [1]

#### Iron Ward (4)
- **Tags**: Buff
- **Class**: Skill Gems

#### Reaper's Invocation (14)
- **Tags**: Buff
- **Class**: Meta Skill Gem
- **Requires**: Requires: Level (1—90), (4—86) Dex, (4—86) Int
